This article focuses on the complexities associated\nwith ocular ciliopathies \u2013 a class of debilitating disorders of the eye caused by ciliary\ndysfunction. Ciliated cell types have been identified in both the anterior and posterior segments\nof the eye. Photoreceptors (rods and cones) are the most studied ciliated neurons in the\nretina, which is located in the posterior eye. The photoreceptors contain a specialized lightsensing\nouter segment, or cilium. Any defects in the development or maintenance of the outer\nsegment can result in severe retinal ciliopathies, such as retinitis pigmentosa and Leber congenital\namaurosis. A role of cilia in the cell types involved in regulating aqueous fluid outflow\nin the anterior segment of the eye has also been recognized. Defects in these cell types are\nfrequently associated with some forms of glaucoma. Here, we will discuss the significance of\nunderstanding the genetic heterogeneity and the pathogenesis of ocular ciliopathies to develop\nsuitable treatment strategies for these blinding disorders.</jats:p>\n</jats:sec>", "DOI": "10.2174/0929867325666180917102557", "type": "journal-article", "created": {"date-parts": [[2018, 9, 17]], "date-time": "2018-09-17T11:52:04Z", "timestamp": 1537185124000}, "page": "3120-3131", "update-policy": "http://dx.doi.org/10.2174/bsp_crossmark_policy", "source": "Crossref", "is-referenced-by-count": 2, "title": ["Ocular Ciliopathies: Genetic and Mechanistic Insights into Developing Therapies"], "prefix": "10.2174", "volume": "26", "author": [{"given": "Mahesh", "family": "Shivanna", "sequence": "first", "affiliation": [{"name": "School of Optometry, Massachusetts College of Pharmacy and Health Sciences University, Worcester, MA, United States"}]}, {"given": "Manisha", "family": "Anand", "sequence": "additional", "affiliation": [{"name": "UMASS Medical School, Worcester, MA 01605, United States"}]}, {"given": "Subhabrata", "family": "Chakrabarti", "sequence": "additional", "affiliation": [{"name": "Brien Holden Eye Research Centre, L.V.
